<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Canadian Yellow Peas" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Plant_Protein_Blend_-CANADIAN_YELLOW_PEAS-min.png?v=1670909055"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Canadian Yellow Peas</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">A sustainably sourced a plant-based protein that is rich in essential amino acids. Yellow peas contain pigments called carotenoids, which give them their yellow color. Yellow pea protein is high in iron, potassium, and magnesium, which are essential minerals that play important roles in maintaining overall health, building, and preserving lean muscle.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Organic Sprouted Brown Rice Protein" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Plant_Protein_Blend_-_ORGANIC_SPROUTED_BROWN_RICE-min.png?v=1670909055"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Organic Sprouted Brown Rice Protein</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">Having a complimentary amino acid profile to peas, rice protein has been scientifically demonstrated build and maintain lean muscle mass comparable to animal proteins. Sprouting brown rice helps to reduce the levels of phytic acid and other compounds that can interfere with the absorption of nutrients as well as making it easier to digest.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Sugar Beet (Palatinose)" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Metabolic_and_Weight_Control_Blend_-_Palatinose_Sugar_Beet-min.png?v=1674450541"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Sugar Beet (Palatinose)</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">Palatinose from sugar beets helps support metabolic health and weight loss. It is a natural source of energy and helps keep you feeling fuller for longer. It also helps reduce the risk of metabolic syndrome, a group of conditions that increase your risk of heart disease, stroke, and type 2 diabetes.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Flaxseed" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Metabolic_and_Weight_Control_Blend_-_FLAXSEED.png?v=1671682972"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Flaxseed</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">Flaxseed is a good source of fiber, which can help control hunger levels and aid weight loss. Fiber can help you feel full longer and avoid overeating. Additionally, flaxseed is a good source of essential fatty acids, which can help protect your heart health by helping to reduce bad cholesterol levels and inflammation.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Inositol" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Metabolic_and_Weight_Control_Blend_-_Inositol-min.png?v=1674450540"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Inositol</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">Inositol is a type of sugar molecule that is found in the body in small amounts. Inositol is important for the body because it is a mineral nutrient and it helps to regulate blood sugar levels.</p>
</div>
</div>

<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Vitamin D3" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Vitashine_Vitamin_D3.png?v=1671685038"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Vitamin D3</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Vitamin D is an essential nutrient that is important for many functions in the body. Vitamin D deficiency is common in modern lifestyles. It is important for maintaining healthy bones and muscles. It plays a role in regulating the amount of calcium and phosphorus in the body, which are both essential for strong bones and boosting the immune system.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Vitamin K2" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Vitamin_K2-min.png?v=1674452851"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Vitamin K2</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Vitamin K2 is an often overlooked essential micronutrient. It plays an important role in cardiovascular and bone health by helping to remove calcium from the arteries and shuttle it into the bones where it belongs. Vitamin K2 also supports the immune system by boosting the production of antibodies and enhancing the function of the immune system's cells.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Magnesium" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Magnesium-min.png?v=1674452898"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Magnesium</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Magnesium is an essential mineral that plays a key role in many bodily functions. Magnesium is involved in energy production, protein synthesis, and muscle function. Magnesium helps the body convert food into energy and plays a role in the contraction and relaxation of muscles.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Zinc" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Zinc.png?v=1670994123"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Zinc</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Zinc helps the body repair damaged tissues, which is especially important for athletes who often put their bodies under a great deal of stress and strain. Without enough zinc, athletes may experience a reduced ability to perform at their best and may be more susceptible to illness and injury.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Choline" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Choline.png?v=1671685037"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Choline</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Choline is a nutrient that is important for brain health. It helps to make acetylcholine, a neurotransmitter that is important for memory and learning. Choline is also important for the production of red blood cells.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Vitamin B12" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Methylated_Vitality_B12.png?v=1671685038"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Vitamin B12</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            B12 is a water soluble vitamin that is essential for the body’s energy production. B12 supplementation is important for vegans and plant-based dieters who do not get enough through the diet. High doses of B12 may help to support cognitive function and a strong immune system.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Selenium" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Essential_Micronutrients_-_Selenium-min.png?v=1674453021"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Selenium</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Selenium is important for the body because it helps promote the health of the thyroid gland and the reproductive system. The loss of nutrients in soil has resulted in a decrease of selenium levels in food, leading to rising incidences of selenium deficiency, a known cause of thyroid disorders.
          </p>

<div class="gm-vlign"></div>

<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Lipase is an enzyme that helps break down fat in the body. Lipase is an enzyme that helps your body break down lipids, including triglycerides. This is important because it helps to remove dangerous substances from your bloodstream and prevent the accumulation of fat in tissue.
          </p>

<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Protease" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_Protease.png?v=1670910919"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Protease</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            The enzyme protease plays a crucial role in the digestive process by breaking down the proteins found in food into their component amino acids, which can then be absorbed and used by the body for various metabolic processes.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Lactobacillus Acidophilus" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_Lactobacillus_Acidophilus.png?v=1671685550"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Lactobacillus Acidophilus</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Lactobacillus acidophilus is a type of beneficial bacteria that is commonly found in the human gut, as well as in fermented foods like yogurt and kefir. It is considered a "probiotic" because it can help maintain the balance of good bacteria in the gut and provide various health benefits.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Lactobacillus Plantarum" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_LACTOBACILLUS_PLANTARUM.png?v=1671685548"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Lactobacillus Plantarum</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            This beneficial strain of gut-boosting bacteria plays an important role in nutrient absorption, immune function and fighting off infections. The lactobacillus genus of probiotics are found in many fermented foods like pickles, sauerkraut, and kimchi.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Lactobacillus Rhamosus" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_LACTOBACILLUS_RHAMOSUS-min.png?v=1674453791"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Lactobacillus Rhamnosus</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            In addition to having similar benefits as other lactobacilli, L. rhamnosus is also thought to play a role in maintaining the integrity of the gut barrier, which helps to keep harmful substances out of the body and prevent inflammation. This is important for overall gut health and may also play a role in preventing certain chronic conditions.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Bifidobacterium Breve" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_BIFIDOBACTERIUM_BREVE.png?v=1671685548"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Bifidobacterium Breve</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Probiotics, such as those in the Bifidobacterium families, have been studied for their potential role in weight management. Bifidobacterium breve is one type of probiotic that may help to shift the balance of gut bacteria towards a more favorable composition, which may impact weight, regulate hunger hormones and improve metabolism.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Bifidobacterium  " src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Digestive_Blend_-_BIFIDOBACTERIUM_LONGUM.png?v=1671685548"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Bifidobacterium Longum</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Bifidobacterium is another beneficial probiotic that may help to manage certain skin conditions and has shown promising results for having a beneficial effect on mental health, specifically on anxiety and depression symptoms.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Pomegranate" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Longevity_Blend_-_Pomegranate_Seeds.png?v=1671685356"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Pomegranate</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Urolithin A is a compound that is produced in the human gut when certain types of ellagitannins, found in pomegranate, are metabolized by the gut microbiome. Over 100+ studies have suggested that urolithin A may support longevity by improving mitochondria health and supporting the production of ATP - the primary molecule for energy storage &amp; transfer in cells.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Grapeseed" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Longevity_Blend_-_Grapeseed_Extract.png?v=1671685355"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Grapeseed</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            Grape seed is a good source of antioxidants, including resveratrol, which has been shown to protect cells from damage and may help keep the brain healthy as we age. Grape seed also contains vitamins A, C, and E, as well as minerals such as potassium, magnesium, and zinc. These nutrients may help keep the body healthy and may help to improve overall longevity.
          </p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div class="swiper-slide">
<div class="gm-swiper-content">
<div class="gm-swiper-content-left">
<img alt="Co-Q10" src="https://cdn.shopify.com/s/files/1/2001/9829/files/Longevity_Blend_-_Coenzyme_Q10.png?v=1671685356"/>
</div>
<div class="gm-swiper-content-right">
<div class="gm-swiper-title">Co-Q10</div>
<div class="gm-vlign"></div>
<p class="gm-swiper-text">
            CoQ-10 is a key component of the electron transport chain in the body. It helps to create energy in the body by helping to convert food into energy. It is found in the bloodstream and is used by the body to make new cells.
          </p>
</div>
